--- Commit Message ---
LU-15012 llite: Unreplayed open leads to version mismatch

Uncommitted close removes open from replay list.
So unlink from another client destroys the file
and all other requests the file fail with version checking.

Keep open in replay list until close is committed.

Change-Id: Ie57645ff6e661fa9cf51b1dad56377426661e1b5
HPE-bug-id: LUS-9298, LUS-9367, LUS-9500, LUS-10185, LUS-10208, LUS-12086

Signed-off-by: Andriy Skulysh <andriy.skulysh@hpe.com>
